<script type="text/javascript">
    if (typeof TiaraTracker !== 'undefined') {
        TiaraTracker.getInstance().init({
            svcDomain: window.location.hostname,
            disableQuery: true,
            enableHash: false,
            deployment: "production"
        });
    }

    window.Tiara = {
        setSection: function(sectionName) {
            if (typeof TiaraTracker === 'undefined') return;
            TiaraTracker.getInstance().setSection(sectionName);
        },
        trackPage: function(pageId, actionName) {
            if (typeof TiaraTracker === 'undefined') return;
            if (!pageId) {
                if (typeof window.Raven !== 'undefined') {
                    window.Raven.captureException(new Error("pageId is empty"))
                }
                pageId = "empty-page-id"
            }
            actionName = typeof actionName === 'undefined' ? pageId : actionName;
            TiaraTracker.getInstance()
                .setPage(pageId)
                .trackPage(actionName)
                .track();
        }
    }
</script>
